11、
create or replace view v_zc_eb_xunjia_baojia_summary as
select
       b.supplier_code,
       b.supplier_name,
       b.bj_code,
       p.pack_code,
       b.proj_code,
       min(bd.gong_huo_date) as PROMISE_WORK_DATE,
       sum(bd.sp_total_sum) as bid_sum
  from zc_eb_xunjia_baojia        b,
       zc_eb_xunjia_baojia_detail bd,
       zc_eb_xunjia_baojia_pack   p
 where b.bj_code = bd.bj_code
   and b.bj_code = p.bj_code
   and b.status='1'
   and p.status='2'
   group by b.bj_code,b.proj_code,p.pack_code,b.supplier_code,b.supplier_name;

--2013-07-25-----------------------------------------
1、启用批办单触发器，自动写入需求，需求不在由单位填写
CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER TRIGGER_ZC_EB_DUTY_AUDIT_SHEET
 BEFORE UPDATE ON ZC_EB_DUTY_AUDIT_SHEET
 FOR EACH ROW

DECLARE
  V_DATACOUNT NUMBER;
  V_REQ_SEQ   VARCHAR(30);
BEGIN
  IF (:NEW.STATUS = 'exec') THEN
    SELECT COUNT(*)
      INTO V_DATACOUNT
      FROM ZC_EB_REQUIREMENT
     WHERE ZC_EB_REQUIREMENT.SN = :NEW.SN;
    IF (V_DATACOUNT = 0) THEN
      SELECT ZC_SEQ_REQUIREMENT.NEXTVAL INTO V_REQ_SEQ FROM DUAL;
      INSERT INTO ZC_EB_REQUIREMENT
        (REQ_CODE, STATUS, PROCESS_INST_ID, SN, REMARK, AGENCY, ORG_CODE)
      VALUES
        (V_REQ_SEQ,
         '0',
         NULL,
         :NEW.SN,
         '',
         :NEW.AGENCY,
         :NEW.SUPERINTENDENT_ORG);

      INSERT INTO ZC_EB_REQUIREMENT_DETAIL
        (DETAIL_CODE,
         REQ_CODE,
         SND,
         SN,
         ZC_YEAR,
         ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,
         ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,
         NAME,
         ARR_DATE,
         BASE_REQ,
         ITEM_ATTACH,
         ITEM_ATTACH_BLOBID,
         NUM,
         ITEM_SUM,
         MER_PRICE,
         PAY_COND,
         SERVICE_PROMISES,
         TYPE,
         DESCRIPTION)
        SELECT ZC_SEQ_REQUIREMENT_DETAIL.NEXTVAL,
               V_REQ_SEQ,
               SND,
               SN,
               ZC_YEAR,
               ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,
               ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,
               ZC_PITEM_NAME,
               ZC_PITEM_ARR_DATE,
               ZC_BASE_GGYQ,
               ZC_PITEM_ATTACH,
               ZC_PITEM_ATTACH_BLOBID,
               ZC_CAIG_NUM,
               ZC_ITEM_SUM,
               ZC_MER_PRICE,
               '',
               '',
               '1',
               ''
          FROM ZC_EB_ENTRUST_DETAIL
         WHERE SN = :NEW.SN;
   /* ELSE
      UPDATE ZC_EB_REQUIREMENT
         SET AGENCY   = :NEW.AGENCY,
             ORG_CODE = :NEW.SUPERINTENDENT_ORG
       WHERE SN = :NEW.SN;*/
    END IF;
  END IF;
END TRIGGER_ZC_EB_DUTY_AUDIT_SHEET;



--2013-07-26-----------------------------------------
1、创建视图，获取正常的分包
 create or replace view v_zc_normal_pack as
  select vp.*
               from zc_v_pro_pack vp
              where vp.pack_code not in
                    (SELECT pack.PACK_CODE
                       from ZC_EB_PACK pack
                      where pack.Status = '5'
                        AND pack.Status = 'cancel'
                     union
                     select qp.packcode
                       from zc_eb_question q, zc_eb_question_pack qp
                      where q.id = qp.id
                        and q.ques_type = '1'
                        and q.handle_mode = '4'
                        and q.state = 'exec')
                        
                        
2、修改视图zc_v_pro_pack，增加zc_make_code
create or replace view zc_v_pro_pack as
select  p.pack_code,
        p.proj_code,
        p.PUR_TYPE,
        p.pack_name,
        p.co_code,
        p.pack_budget,
        p.nd,
        e.zc_make_code
 from zc_eb_pack p,zc_eb_entrust e
 where
 p.entrust_code=e.sn
 and
 p.pack_code not in
 (select c2.pack_code from zc_eb_proj_chg c1,zc_eb_proj_chg_pack c2
  where c1.chg_id=c2.chg_id and c1.status='exec'
 )
union
select c2.pack_code,
       c2.proj_code,
       c2.pur_way,
       c2.pack_name,
       c1.co_code,
       c2.pack_budget,
       c1.nd,
       e.zc_make_code
from zc_eb_proj_chg c1, zc_eb_proj_chg_pack c2,zc_eb_pack p,zc_eb_entrust e
where c1.chg_id=c2.chg_id and c1.status='exec'
and c2.pack_code=p.pack_code
and p.entrust_code=e.sn;

3、修改视图 增加单位名称
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_ZC_P_PRO_MAKE AS
SELECT CHG.PROJ_CODE  PROJ_CODE, ---计划编号
 CHG.PROJ_NAME  PROJ_NAME, ---计划名称
 CHG.CO_CODE    CO_CODE, ----预算单位代码
 CHG.CO_NAME    CO_NAME, ----预算单位
 CHG.PROJ_SUM, ---上次变更金额。
 CHG.Nd         ND, ---预算年度
 CHG.MANAGER, ---采购计划录入人代码（经办人代码）
 CHG.Input_Date, --采购计划录入时间。
 CHG.Pur_Type, ---上次变更采购方式。
 CHG.CHG_ID, ---变更单号
 CHG.Pack_Name,---上次变更内容。
 CHG.ORG_CODE ORG_CODE,
 CHG.Agency,
 'exec' status
 From ZC_EB_PROJ_CHG CHG
 where CHG.Chg_Id not in
 (select CHG1.PROJ_SRC_CODE from ZC_EB_PROJ_CHG CHG1) -- 取末级别的变更记录。
 AND CHG.Status = 'exec' --获取终审通过的

 union
 SELECT make.zc_make_code PROJ_CODE, ---计划编号
 make.zc_make_name PROJ_NAME, ---计划名称
 make.co_code CO_CODE, ---预算单位代码
 M.CO_NAME,
 (make.zc_money_bi_sum -
 (select nvl(sum(CHG2.Proj_Sum), 0)
 from ZC_EB_PROJ_CHG CHG2
 where CHG2.Proj_Src_Code = make.zc_make_code
 and CHG2.Status = 'exec')) as PROJ_SUM,
 make.nd ND, ---预算年度
 make.zc_input_code MANAGER, --采购计划录入人代码
 make.zc_input_date INPUT_DATE, --采购计划录入时间
 make.zc_pifu_cgfs PUR_TYPE, --批复采购方式
 null,
 null,
 make.ORG_CODE,
 make.agency,
 make.zc_make_status
 FROM Zc_p_Pro_Make make,MA_COMPANY M
 where make.zc_fukuan_type='Z01'
 AND MAKE.CO_CODE=M.CO_CODE
 AND MAKE.ND=M.ND
 and (make.zc_money_bi_sum = 0
 or (make.zc_money_bi_sum -
 (select nvl(sum(CHG2.Proj_Sum), 0)
 from ZC_EB_PROJ_CHG CHG2
 where CHG2.Proj_Src_Code = make.zc_make_code
 and CHG2.Status = 'exec')) > 0);

7、修改视图，调整采购方式,并增加 p.executor_name as MANAGER
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_ZC_ZTB_PROJECT AS
SELECT P.PROJ_CODE,
 P.PROJ_NAME,
 P.PROJ_SUM,
 (SELECT VAL
 FROM AS_VAL
 WHERE VALSET_ID = 'ZC_VS_PITEM_OPIWAY'
 AND VAL_ID = P.PUR_TYPE) PUR_TYPE,
 EP.Doc_Seller,
 P.EXECUTOR as MANAGER_CODE,
 p.executor_name as MANAGER,
 P.PROJ_DATE,
 P.IS_SPLIT_PACK,
 P.PHONE,
 P.EMAIL,
 P.FAX,
 A.ZC_AGEY_CODE,
 A.ZC_AGEY_NAME,
 to_char(EP.BID_END_TIME,'yyyy-mm-dd hh24:mi:ss') BID_END_TIME,
 to_char(EP.OPEN_BID_TIME,'yyyy-mm-dd hh24:mi:ss') OPEN_BID_TIME,
 EP.OPEN_BID_ADDRESS,--添加新的开标地址
 P.STATUS,
 (SELECT OPT_VAL
 FROM AS_OPTION
 WHERE OPT_ID = 'OPT_ZC_EB_OUT_WEB_SERVER_IP_ADDRESS') OUT_WEB_SERVER_IP_ADDRESS,
 (SELECT OPT_VAL
 FROM AS_OPTION
 WHERE OPT_ID = 'OPT_ZC_EB_ZTB_FILE_ASKFOR_SOFTINFO') ZTB_FILE_ASKFOR_SOFTINFO,
 (SELECT OPT_VAL
 FROM AS_OPTION
 WHERE OPT_ID = 'OPT_ZC_EB_OUT_WEB_SERVER_TB_PATH') OUT_WEB_SERVER_TB_PATH,
 (SELECT OPT_VAL
 FROM AS_OPTION
 WHERE OPT_ID = 'OPT_ZC_EB_ENCODE_DEMAND') ENCODE_DEMAND,
 (SELECT COUNT(ZBF.PROJ_CODE) FROM ZC_EB_PROJ_ZBFILE ZBF JOIN AS_FILE F ON ZBF.FILE_ID=F.FILE_ID WHERE ZBF.PROJ_CODE=P.PROJ_CODE) IS_HAVE_ZBFILE
 FROM ZC_EB_PROJ P, ZC_B_AGENCY A, ZC_EB_PLAN EP
 WHERE P.AGENCY = A.ZC_AGEY_CODE
 AND EP.PROJ_CODE = P.PROJ_CODE
 AND P.PUR_TYPE IN('1','3','4','6');

1、给zc_eb_formula建立主键
先要删除几条垃圾数据才能执行:
delete from zc_eb_formula f where f.formula_code='ZBJ_2011_10_000089';

delete from zc_eb_formula_item i where i.formula_code='ZBJ_2011_10_000089';

delete from zc_eb_formula_param p where p.formula_code='ZBJ_2011_10_000089';

delete from zc_eb_formula_pack k where k.formula_code='ZBJ_2011_10_000089';

alter table ZC_EB_FORMULA
  add constraint ZC_EB_FORMULA_pk primary key (FORMULA_CODE, PROJ_CODE, PACK_CODE);


2、给ZC_EB_FORMULA_ITEM建立主键
alter table ZC_EB_FORMULA_ITEM
  add constraint ZC_EB_FORMULA_ITEM_pk primary key (ITEM_CODE);

3.新建表ZC_EB_FORMULA_PACK
create table ZC_EB_FORMULA_PACK
(
  PACK_CODE    VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
  FORMULA_CODE VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL,
  PROJ_CODE    VARCHAR2(20) NOT NULL
)
tablespace zfcg
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );
-- Add comments to the table 
comment on table ZC_EB_FORMULA_PACK
  is '指标级和分包关联';
-- Create/Recreate primary, unique and foreign key constraints 
alter table ZC_EB_FORMULA_PACK
  add constraint FORMULA_PACK_KEY primary key (PACK_CODE, FORMULA_CODE,proj_code)
  using index 
  tablespace zfcg
  pctfree 10
  initrans 2
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

6.
-- Create table
create table ZC_QXQB
(
  qxqb_code           VARCHAR2(60) not null,
  co_code             VARCHAR2(60),
  excutor             VARCHAR2(60),
  excutor_name        VARCHAR2(100),
  input_date          DATE,
  supplier            VARCHAR2(60),
  supplier_name       VARCHAR2(200),
  co_name             VARCHAR2(200),
  su_bank_account     VARCHAR2(200),
  su_bank             VARCHAR2(200),
  su_bank_shoukuanren VARCHAR2(200),
  nd                  VARCHAR2(10),
  qxqb_sum            NUMBER,
  remark              VARCHAR2(1000),
  status              VARCHAR2(10),
  qxqb_type           VARCHAR2(10)
)
tablespace ZFCG
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );
-- Add comments to the table 
comment on table ZC_QXQB
  is '汽修汽保';
-- Add comments to the columns 
comment on column ZC_QXQB.excutor
  is '录入人';
comment on column ZC_QXQB.excutor_name
  is '录入人名称';
comment on column ZC_QXQB.input_date
  is '录入时间';
comment on column ZC_QXQB.supplier
  is '供应商';
comment on column ZC_QXQB.su_bank_account
  is '银行账号';
comment on column ZC_QXQB.su_bank
  is '开户行';
comment on column ZC_QXQB.su_bank_shoukuanren
  is '银行收款人';
comment on column ZC_QXQB.qxqb_sum
  is '金额';
comment on column ZC_QXQB.qxqb_type
  is '1 汽修 ； 2 汽保';
-- Create/Recreate primary, unique and foreign key constraints 
alter table ZC_QXQB
  add constraint ZC_QXQB_PK primary key (QXQB_CODE)
  using index 
  tablespace ZFCG
  pctfree 10
  initrans 2
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

1.
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION newid RETURN VARCHAR2 IS
  guid VARCHAR2(38);
BEGIN
  guid  := SYS_guid();
RETURN '{'||substr(guid,1,8)||'-'|| substr(guid,9,4)||'-'|| substr(guid,13,4)||'-'|| substr(guid,17,4)||'-'||

substr(guid,21,12)|| '}';
END newid;
2.
create or replace view vw_budget_shouru as 
--单位收入表，支付时，必须有收入才可以支付，但资金性质是经费拨款(001001)的不受收入控制，可以支付
select b.en_code, nvl(sum(a.avi_money),0) as shouru,b.set_year
  from gfmis.gl_balance a, gfmis.gl_ccids b
 where a.ccid = b.ccid
   and a.account_id = '{EFBE38D0-9FDE-11DD-9348-9F61509BF608}'--资金性质是经费拨款(001001)的不受收入控制，其他类型资金必须受收入控制，无收入不能付款
 group by b.en_code,b.set_year;

7.
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW ZC_V_OPEN_BID AS
SELECT P.PROJ_CODE,
 P.PROJ_NAME,
 PACK.PACK_CODE,
 PACK.PACK_NAME,
 S.PROVIDER_CODE,
 S.PROVIDER_NAME,
 S.SIGNUP_ID,
 C.SIGNUP_PACK_ID,
 C.BID_SUM,
 C.BID_DOC_ID,
 C.BID_DOC_NAME,
 C.ECBJ_SUM,
 C.TBYLB_FILE_ID,
 C.TBYLB_FILE_NAME,
 C.PROMISE_WORK_DATE,
 (CASE
 WHEN C.OPEN_BID_STATUS IN ('1', '2') THEN
 '' || C.BID_SUM
 ELSE
 '******'
 END) AS BID_SUM_MASK,
 CASE
 WHEN c.open_bid_status IS NULL THEN
 '0'
 ELSE
 c.open_bid_status
 END AS OPEN_BID_STATUS,
 C.OPEN_BID_REMARK,
 C.OPEN_BID_DATE,
 C.IS_PAY_GUARANTEE,
 C.IS_SUBMIT_BID_DOC,
 P.AGENCY,
 P.Org_Code,
 P.ND
 FROM ZC_EB_PROJ P, ZC_EB_PACK PACK, ZC_EB_SIGNUP S, ZC_EB_SIGNUP_PACK C
 WHERE P.PROJ_CODE = PACK.PROJ_CODE
 AND PACK.PACK_CODE = C.PACK_CODE
 AND P.PROJ_CODE = S.PROJ_CODE
 AND S.SIGNUP_ID = C.SIGNUP_ID
 AND C.IS_PAY_GUARANTEE in ('1','2')
 AND   C.IS_SUBMIT_BID_DOC='Y'
 AND PACK.STATUS in('0','1','2','3','4')
 ORDER BY C.OPEN_BID_DATE DESC;

--20131201---------------
--1
create or replace function getWorkDay(sellEndDate in date, days in int)
  return date is
  Result    date;
  times     varchar2(8);
  chinaDate VARCHAR2(20);
  i         int := 2;
  cursor c01 is
    select CHINA_DATE
      from zc_sys_work_day
     where CHINA_DATE > to_char(sellEndDate, 'yyyy-mm-dd')
       and date_type = 0
     order by china_date;
begin
  if sellEndDate is null then
    return null;
   end if;
  times := to_char(sysdate, 'hh24:mi:SS');
  open c01;
  loop
    fetch c01
      into chinaDate;
    EXIT WHEN c01%NOTFOUND or i > days;
    i := i + 1;
  end loop;
  close c01;
  Result := to_Date(trim(chinaDate) || ' ' || times,
                    'yyyy-mm-dd hh24:mi:SS');
  return(Result);
end getWorkDay;

--2
-- Create table
create table ZC_SYS_WORK_DAY
(
  set_year   NUMBER(4) not null,
  date_month VARCHAR2(20) not null,
  date_day   VARCHAR2(2) not null,
  week       NUMBER,
  date_type  NUMBER,
  china_date VARCHAR2(20),
  last_ver   VARCHAR2(30)
)
tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

create table ZC_JZ_MAKE_TEMP
(
  zc_make_code VARCHAR2(128),
  zc_bi_no     VARCHAR2(64),
  zc_jhua_sum  NUMBER(16,2) default 0,
  zc_ht_sum    NUMBER(16,2) default 0,
  zc_bal_sum   NUMBER(16,3) default 0
)
tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

--13
create or replace procedure sp_zc_jiChuZiLiaoJieZhuan(curNd in varchar2) is
begin
  --结转as_emp_position
  delete from as_emp_position where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_emp_position
  select emp_code, posi_code, org_code, co_code, emp_posi_id, nd+1, sysdate from as_emp_position where nd=curNd;

--结转as_org
  delete from as_org where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_org 
  select co_code, org_code, org_name, parent_org_code, is_lowest, quic_code, prin_code, linkman, tele, org_id, org_type_code, nd+1, is_need_send_bank, sysdate, SYS_GUID(), trigger_enable from as_org where nd=curNd;

--结转as_org_position
  delete from as_org_position where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_org_position 
  select co_code, posi_code, org_code, leader_posi_id, org_posi_id, nd+1, sysdate from as_org_position where nd=curNd;
 
--结转 as_wf_business_superior
/*delete from as_wf_business_superior where nd=curNd+1;
insert into as_wf_business_superior
select id, jun_co_code, jun_org_code, jun_posi_code, jun_emp_code, sup_condition, sup_co_code, sup_org_code, sup_posi_code, sup_emp_code, project_name, description, priority, nd+1 from as_wf_business_superior where nd=curNd;
*/
--结转 ma_company
delete from ma_company where nd=curNd+1;
insert into ma_company
select co_code, co_type_code, gb_code, co_name, co_fullna, quic_code, mark, post_code, comm_addr, address, url, link_man, co_clerk, co_leader, fi_leader, loca_tele, director_code, parent_co_code, f_co_code, is_used, f_org_code, is_self, bank_acc, shop_card_no, corp_repr, trade_name, country, province, city, real_co_code, is_lowest, nd+1, fina_level, co_kind, is_pilot, is_need_send_bank, region_code, sysdate, is_need_send_bank_sl, co_type_code_1, can_getbill, getbill_id, can_charge, turn_in_acct, nt_acc_id, nt_acc_name, nt_hesuan_co_code, sys_guid(), trigger_enable, pr_bi_cocode from ma_company where nd=curNd;

--结转 ZC_B_CATALOGUE
delete  from ZC_B_CATALOGUE where zc_year=curNd+1;
insert into ZC_B_CATALOGUE 
select zc_year+1, zc_catalogue_code, zc_catalogue_name, zc_catalogue_code_par, zc_catalogue_type, zc_quota, zc_metric_unit, zc_is_vital, zc_is_used, zc_target_type, zc_pinmu_ctlg, zc_is_cgzx_zg, zc_is_general, zc_year, zc_diyu_daima, zc_quota_unit, zc_cg_leixing, zc_zcgz_std, zc_is_assert, zc_catalogue_name_par, zc_is_dianzi_toubiao, zc_jj_pp_num, zc_jj_price_quota from zc_b_catalogue where zc_year=curNd;

end sp_zc_jiChuZiLiaoJieZhuan;

--9
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW ZC_VW_ZHONGBIAO AS
SELECT r.proj_code,
               r.proj_name,
               r.pack_code,
               r.pack_name,
               r.provider_name,
               r.PROVIDER_CODE,
               r.pur_type,
               r.REPORT_CODE,
               r.EXECUTOR,
               r.EXECUTOR_NAME,
               r.status,
               r.remark,
               r.RECORD_CODE,
               r.EXECUTE_DATE,
               r.PROCESS_INST_ID,
               r.Nd nd,
               r.BID_LOCATION,
               r.PUR_PEOPLE,
               r.BID_DATE,
               r.IS_GOON_AUDIT,
               r.BID_SUM,
               r.CO_CODE,
               r.CO_NAME,
               r.ZC_CO_LINKMAN,
               r.AGENCY,
               r.ORG_CODE,
               k.entrust_code
          FROM ZC_EB_EVAL_REPORT r,zc_eb_pack k
         where r.pur_type != '5'
         and r.status!= 'cancel'
         and r.provider_code is not null
         and r.proj_code=k.proj_code
         and r.pack_code=k.pack_code
        union
        select p.proj_code,
               p.proj_name,
               p.pack_code,
               p.pack_name,
               p.WIN_BID_PROVIDER_NAME,
               p.WIN_BID_PROVIDER_CODE,
               '5' pur_type,
               p.RFQ_CODE REPORT_CODE,
               p.CREATOR EXECUTOR,
               p.creator EXECUTOR_name,
               p.status,
               '' remark,
               '' RECORD_CODE,
               p.CREATE_DATE,
               p.PROCESS_INST_ID,
               p.Nd nd,
               '' BID_LOCATION,
               '' PUR_PEOPLE,
               p.OPEN_BID_DATE,
               p.IS_GOON_AUDIT,
               p.WIN_BID_SUM,
               e.co_code,
               m.co_name,
               m.link_man,
               p.AGENCY,
               p.ORG_CODE,
               k.entrust_code
          from zc_eb_rfq_pack p, zc_eb_pack k, zc_eb_entrust e, ma_company m
         where p.pack_code = k.pack_code
           and k.entrust_code = e.sn
           and e.co_code = m.co_code
           and e.nd = m.nd
           and p.status!= 'cancel'
           and p.win_bid_provider_code is not null

--14
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_ZC_NORMAL_PACK AS
select vp."PACK_CODE",vp."PROJ_CODE",vp."PUR_TYPE",vp."PACK_NAME",vp."CO_CODE",vp."PACK_BUDGET",vp."ND",vp."ZC_MAKE_CODE"
               from zc_v_pro_pack vp
              where vp.pack_code not in
                    (SELECT pack.PACK_CODE
                       from ZC_EB_PACK pack
                      where pack.Status = '5'
                        or pack.Status = 'cancel'
                     union
                     select qp.packcode
                       from zc_eb_question q, zc_eb_question_pack qp
                      where q.id = qp.id
                        and q.ques_type = '1'
                        and q.handle_mode = '4'
                        and q.state = 'exec');
                        
-------20140307----------------------------
--1
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_ZC_FA_TYPE AS
SELECT "FATYPE_CODE","FATYPE_NAME","RESI_RAT","USE_LIFE","PARENT_FATYPE_CODE","IS_LOWEST","FASTAT_CODE","FATYPE_SORE","FATYPE_DW","IS_SIMPLE","IS_SPECIAL_TYPE" FROM FA.FA_TYPE;

--2
create or replace view v_zc_fa_cardstyl_type as
select a.fatype_code, b.card_styl_code
  from FA.fa_type a,
       (select fatype_code, card_styl_code from FA.FA_CARDSTYL_TYPE) b
 where a.fatype_code like (b.fatype_code || '%');
 
--3
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_ZC_FA_CARD_STYLD AS
SELECT "CARD_STYL_CODE","FAITEM_CODE","FAITEM_NAME","COL_INDEX","ROW_INDEX","IS_RO","IS_VISI","IS_NULL","IS_MODIFY" FROM FA.FA_CARD_STYLD;

--4
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_ZC_FA_USERS AS SELECT * FROM FA.FA_USERS

--5
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_ZC_FA_ORG_VIEW AS
SELECT CO_CODE,
       ORG_CODE,
       ORG_NAME,
       ND,
       DECODE(ORG_PARENT_CODE, 0, '', ORG_PARENT_CODE) ORG_PARENT_CODE,
       IS_FOLIAGE
  FROM FA.FA_ORG_TRANS
 WHERE IS_FOLIAGE = 'Y';

-------------------20140313----------------------------
--1
create or replace procedure sp_zc_jiChuZiLiaoJieZhuan(curNd in varchar2) is
begin
  --结转as_emp_position
  delete from as_emp_position where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_emp_position
  select emp_code, posi_code, org_code, co_code, emp_posi_id, nd+1, sysdate from as_emp_position where nd=curNd;

--结转as_org
  delete from as_org where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_org 
  select co_code, org_code, org_name, parent_org_code, is_lowest, quic_code, prin_code, linkman, tele, org_id, org_type_code, nd+1, is_need_send_bank, sysdate, SYS_GUID(), trigger_enable from as_org where nd=curNd;

--结转as_org_position
  delete from as_org_position where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_org_position 
  select co_code, posi_code, org_code, leader_posi_id, org_posi_id, nd+1, sysdate from as_org_position where nd=curNd;
 
--结转 as_wf_business_superior

*/
--结转 ma_company
delete from ma_company where nd=curNd+1;
insert into ma_company
select co_code, co_type_code, gb_code, co_name, co_fullna, quic_code, mark, post_code, comm_addr, address, url, link_man, co_clerk, co_leader, fi_leader, loca_tele, director_code, parent_co_code, f_co_code, is_used, f_org_code, is_self, bank_acc, shop_card_no, corp_repr, trade_name, country, province, city, real_co_code, is_lowest, nd+1, fina_level, co_kind, is_pilot, is_need_send_bank, region_code, sysdate, is_need_send_bank_sl, co_type_code_1, can_getbill, getbill_id, can_charge, turn_in_acct, nt_acc_id, nt_acc_name, nt_hesuan_co_code, sys_guid(), trigger_enable, pr_bi_cocode from ma_company where nd=curNd;

--结转 ZC_B_CATALOGUE
delete  from ZC_B_CATALOGUE where zc_year=curNd+1;
insert into ZC_B_CATALOGUE 
select zc_year+1, zc_catalogue_code, zc_catalogue_name, zc_catalogue_code_par, zc_catalogue_type, zc_quota, zc_metric_unit, zc_is_vital, zc_is_used, zc_target_type, zc_pinmu_ctlg, zc_is_cgzx_zg, zc_is_general, zc_year, zc_diyu_daima, zc_quota_unit, zc_cg_leixing, zc_zcgz_std, zc_is_assert, zc_catalogue_name_par, zc_is_dianzi_toubiao, zc_jj_pp_num, zc_jj_price_quota from zc_b_catalogue where zc_year=curNd;

--结转 wf_executor_source
delete  from wf_executor_source where extnd=curNd+1;
insert into wf_executor_source 
select node_id, executor, source, responsibility, extcocode, extorgcode, extnd+1 from wf_executor_source where extnd=curNd;

--结转 as_wf_business_superior
 insert into as_wf_business_superior
    select newid, jun_co_code, jun_org_code, jun_posi_code, jun_emp_code, sup_condition, sup_co_code, sup_org_code, sup_posi_code, sup_emp_code, project_name, description, priority, 2014 from as_wf_business_superior where nd=curNd

end sp_zc_jiChuZiLiaoJieZhuan;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION newid RETURN VARCHAR2 IS
  guid VARCHAR2(38);
BEGIN
  guid  := SYS_guid();
RETURN '{'||substr(guid,1,8)||'-'|| substr(guid,9,4)||'-'|| substr(guid,13,4)||'-'|| substr(guid,17,4)||'-'||

substr(guid,21,12)|| '}';
END newid;

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION newid RETURN VARCHAR2 IS
  guid VARCHAR2(38);
BEGIN
  guid  := SYS_guid();
RETURN '{'||substr(guid,1,8)||'-'|| substr(guid,9,4)||'-'|| substr(guid,13,4)||'-'|| substr(guid,17,4)||'-'||

substr(guid,21,12)|| '}';
END newid;

--4
create or replace procedure sp_zc_jiChuZiLiaoJieZhuan(curNd in varchar2) is
begin
  --结转as_emp_position
  delete from as_emp_position where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_emp_position
  select emp_code, posi_code, org_code, co_code, emp_posi_id, nd+1, sysdate from as_emp_position where nd=curNd;

--结转as_org
  delete from as_org where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_org
  select co_code, org_code, org_name, parent_org_code, is_lowest, quic_code, prin_code, linkman, tele, org_id, org_type_code, nd+1, is_need_send_bank, sysdate, SYS_GUID(), trigger_enable from as_org where nd=curNd;

--结转as_org_position
  delete from as_org_position where nd=curNd+1;
  insert into as_org_position
  select co_code, posi_code, org_code, leader_posi_id, org_posi_id, nd+1, sysdate from as_org_position where nd=curNd;

--结转 as_wf_business_superior
/*delete from as_wf_business_superior where nd=curNd+1;
insert into as_wf_business_superior
select id, jun_co_code, jun_org_code, jun_posi_code, jun_emp_code, sup_condition, sup_co_code, sup_org_code, sup_posi_code, sup_emp_code, project_name, description, priority, nd+1 from as_wf_business_superior where nd=curNd;
*/
--结转 ma_company
delete from ma_company where nd=curNd+1;
insert into ma_company
select co_code, co_type_code, gb_code, co_name, co_fullna, quic_code, mark, post_code, comm_addr, address, url, link_man, co_clerk, co_leader, fi_leader, loca_tele, director_code, parent_co_code, f_co_code, is_used, f_org_code, is_self, bank_acc, shop_card_no, corp_repr, trade_name, country, province, city, real_co_code, is_lowest, nd+1, fina_level, co_kind, is_pilot, is_need_send_bank, region_code, sysdate, is_need_send_bank_sl, co_type_code_1, can_getbill, getbill_id, can_charge, turn_in_acct, nt_acc_id, nt_acc_name, nt_hesuan_co_code, sys_guid(), trigger_enable, pr_bi_cocode from ma_company where nd=curNd;

--结转 ZC_B_CATALOGUE
delete  from ZC_B_CATALOGUE where zc_year=curNd+1;
insert into ZC_B_CATALOGUE
select zc_year+1, zc_catalogue_code, zc_catalogue_name, zc_catalogue_code_par, zc_catalogue_type, zc_quota, zc_metric_unit, zc_is_vital, zc_is_used, zc_target_type, zc_pinmu_ctlg, zc_is_cgzx_zg, zc_is_general, zc_year, zc_diyu_daima, zc_quota_unit, zc_cg_leixing, zc_zcgz_std, zc_is_assert, zc_catalogue_name_par, zc_is_dianzi_toubiao, zc_jj_pp_num, zc_jj_price_quota from zc_b_catalogue where zc_year=curNd;

--结转 wf_executor_source
delete  from wf_executor_source where extnd=curNd+1;
insert into wf_executor_source
select node_id, executor, source, responsibility, extcocode, extorgcode, extnd+1 from wf_executor_source where extnd=curNd;

--结转 as_wf_business_superior
delete  from as_wf_business_superior where nd=curNd+1;
 insert into as_wf_business_superior
    select newid, jun_co_code, jun_org_code, jun_posi_code, jun_emp_code, sup_condition, sup_co_code, sup_org_code, sup_posi_code, sup_emp_code, project_name, description, priority, curNd+1 from as_wf_business_superior where nd=curNd;

end sp_zc_jiChuZiLiaoJieZhuan;

--4
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW ZC_V_MAKE_YEAREND AS
SELECT
       A.co_code,    --单位代码
       A.org_code, --主管处室代码
       A.ZC_MAKE_CODE,  --项目代码
       A.ZC_MAKE_NAME,  --项目名称
       A.ZC_MAKE_STATUS,--项目状态
       A.nd, --预算年度
       A.ZC_YEP_FLAG,   --年终处理标记
       nvl(A.ZC_YEP_SUM,0.00) as ZC_YEP_SUM,    --年终处理金额
       nvl(A.ZC_MONEY_BI_SUM,0.00) as ZC_MONEY_BI_SUM,  --项目预算金额
       nvl(A.ZC_MONEY_BI_YZX,0.00) as ZC_MONEY_BI_YZX,  --已经执行金额
       nvl(A.ZC_MONEY_HT_YBA,0.00) as ZC_MONEY_HT_YBA,  --合同已经备案
       nvl(A.ZC_MONEY_BI_YZX-A.ZC_MONEY_HT_YBA,0.00) AS ZC_MONEY_HT_WQD, --待签合同金额
       nvl(B.ZC_MONEY_BI_YJS,0.00) as ZC_MONEY_BI_YJS,  --已经结算金额
       nvl(A.ZC_MONEY_BI_SUM-A.ZC_MONEY_BI_YZX,0.00) AS ZC_MONEY_BI_KJZ, --可以结转金额（含变更）
       nvl(A.ZC_MONEY_HT_YBA-B.ZC_MONEY_BI_YJS,0.00) AS ZC_MONEY_HT_KLZ,   --可列支(结转)合同金额(合同备案金额-已经结算数)【含待签合同金额】
       nvl(A.ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,0.00) AS ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM, /*合同结转金额*/
       A.PROCESS_INST_ID,
       A.ZC_FUKUAN_TYPE, -- 采购类型；
       A.ZC_MAKE_SEQUENCE, -- 组织形式；
       A.ZC_PITEM_MODE, --采购方式；
       A.ZC_INPUT_DATE

 FROM
       ZC_P_PRO_MAKE A
       LEFT JOIN
         (
         SELECT
            ZC_MAKE_CODE,
            SUM(ZC_BI_YJJS_SUM) AS ZC_MONEY_BI_YJS --已经结算数
         FROM
            ZC_XMCG_HT_BI
         GROUP BY
         ZC_MAKE_CODE
         ) B
       ON A.ZC_MAKE_CODE = B.ZC_MAKE_CODE;

--1
-- Create table
create table ZC_PAY_GK_INFO
(
  zc_bill_type   VARCHAR2(60) not null,
  zc_bill_id     VARCHAR2(60) not null,
  gk_vou_id      VARCHAR2(60) not null,
  gk_return_flag VARCHAR2(2),
  gk_return_date DATE,
  send_gk_date   DATE not null,
  gk_vou_type    VARCHAR2(60)
)
tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );
-- Add comments to the table 
comment on table ZC_PAY_GK_INFO
  is '采购送国库后的关联信息';
-- Add comments to the columns 
comment on column ZC_PAY_GK_INFO.zc_bill_type
  is '采购送国库的单据类型，如合同支付、汽修、汽保等，分别对应不同代码';
comment on column ZC_PAY_GK_INFO.zc_bill_id
  is '采购送国库的单据id';
comment on column ZC_PAY_GK_INFO.gk_vou_id
  is '国库返回的支付单据id，可能是支付申请id，也可以是支付凭证的id，根据GK_VOU_TYPE可以判别';
comment on column ZC_PAY_GK_INFO.gk_return_flag
  is '是否国库退回：Y/N，当支付发生退款/退票等情形时，将这个值治为Y，默认值是N';
comment on column ZC_PAY_GK_INFO.gk_return_date
  is '国库退回时间';
comment on column ZC_PAY_GK_INFO.send_gk_date
  is '采购送国库的时间';
comment on column ZC_PAY_GK_INFO.gk_vou_type
  is '根据OPT_ZC_PAY_IS_ZhiFuPingZhen这个值判断，如果是Y，则是支付凭证(ZFPZ)，否则为支付申请(ZFSQ)';
-- Create/Recreate primary, unique and foreign key constraints 
alter table ZC_PAY_GK_INFO
  add constraint ZC_PAY_GK_INFO_PK primary key (ZC_BILL_TYPE, ZC_BILL_ID, GK_VOU_ID)
  using index 
  tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 2
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

--2
create or replace trigger TRIGGER_ZC_PAY_GK_INFO
  after update on zc_pay_gk_info  
  --如果发生国库退款/退票，则由国库系统执行触发器，往表ZC_PAY_GK_INFO回写状态、退回时间、退回原因									
  --同时触发器TRIGGER_ZC_PAY_GK_INFO将送国库的单据（合同支付、汽修、汽保）等的状态置为gkBack,标明该支付失败了
  for each row
declare
  -- local variables here
begin
  IF :NEW.GK_RETURN_FLAG='Y' OR :NEW.GK_RETURN_FLAG='y' THEN
    IF :NEW.ZC_BILL_TYPE='ZC_BILL_TYPE_HT_ZHIFU' THEN
    UPDATE ZC_P_PRO_BAL B SET B.ZC_BAL_STATUS='gkBack' where b.zc_bal_id=:new.zc_bill_id;
    END IF;
    IF :NEW.ZC_BILL_TYPE='ZC_BILL_TYPE_QX' THEN
      UPDATE ZC_QX X SET X.STATUS='gkBack' where x.qx_code=:new.zc_bill_id;
    END IF;
    IF :NEW.ZC_BILL_TYPE='ZC_BILL_TYPE_QB' THEN
      UPDATE ZC_QB QB SET QB.STATUS='gkBack' WHERE QB.QB_CODE=:NEW.ZC_BILL_ID;
    END IF;
    
  END IF;
end TRIGGER_ZC_PAY_GK_INFO;

------------20140513-----------------------------
--1
create or replace view v_zc_eb_pack_plan as
select pk.pack_code,
       pk.proj_code,
       pl.plan_code,
       pl.sell_start_time,
       nvl(pp.sell_end_time, pl.sell_end_time) sell_end_time,
       nvl(pp.bid_end_time, pl.bid_end_time) bid_end_time,
       nvl(pp.open_bid_time, pl.open_bid_time) open_bid_time,
       pl.open_bid_address,
       pl.nd,
       pl.doc_price,
       pl.doc_seller,
       pl.doc_sell_address,
       pl.doc_sell_phone,
       pl.create_date,
       pl.creator,
       pl.remark,
       pl.process_inst_id
  from zc_eb_pack pk, zc_eb_pack_plan pp, zc_eb_plan pl
 where pk.proj_code = pp.proj_code(+)
   and pk.pack_code = pp.pack_code(+)
   and pk.proj_code = pl.proj_code
   order by proj_code,to_number(pack_code)
   ;

update ZC_EB_TEMPLATE_PARAM p set p.is_man_set='Y';

DROP TABLE ZC_P_PRO_BAL_CHG_BI;
-- Create table
create table ZC_P_PRO_BAL_CHG_BI
(
  zc_make_code        VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_bi_no            VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_bi_sum           NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_bi_jhua_sum      NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_bi_do_sum        NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_bi_yjba_sum      NUMBER(16,2),
  bi_target_code      VARCHAR2(60),
  b_acc_code          VARCHAR2(60),
  b_acc_name          VARCHAR2(200),
  co_code             VARCHAR2(60),
  co_name             VARCHAR2(200),
  dec_money           NUMBER(16,2),
  fund_code           VARCHAR2(60),
  fund_name           VARCHAR2(200),
  inceptdoc_code      VARCHAR2(60),
  inceptdoc_name      VARCHAR2(200),
  manage_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  manage_name         VARCHAR2(200),
  nd                  CHAR(4),
  org_code            VARCHAR2(60),
  org_name            VARCHAR2(100),
  origin_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  origin_name         VARCHAR2(200),
  outlay_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  outlay_name         VARCHAR2(200),
  payout_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  payout_name         VARCHAR2(200),
  paytype_code        VARCHAR2(60),
  paytype_name        VARCHAR2(200),
  project_code        VARCHAR2(60),
  project_name        VARCHAR2(200),
  project_type_code   VARCHAR2(60),
  project_type_name   VARCHAR2(200),
  senddoc_code        VARCHAR2(60),
  senddoc_name        VARCHAR2(200),
  senddoc_type_code   VARCHAR2(60),
  senddoc_type_name   VARCHAR2(200),
  zc_bi_htba_sum      NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_cg_type          VARCHAR2(2),
  zc_plan_type        VARCHAR2(2),
  zc_save_num         NUMBER,
  zc_catalogue_code   VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_catalogue_name   VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_year             VARCHAR2(4),
  zc_yep_sum          NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_bi_apd_flag      VARCHAR2(2000),
  zc_fund_remark      VARCHAR2(500),
  zc_fund_file        VARCHAR2(200),
  zc_fund_file_blobid VARCHAR2(200),
  is_add_onfunds      VARCHAR2(4),
  supplement_amount   NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_pro_bi_seq       VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_use_bi_id        VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_zj_type          VARCHAR2(4),
  gb_name             VARCHAR2(60),
  bt_name             VARCHAR2(60),
  bal_chg_id          VARCHAR2(200) not null,
  zc_bi_yjjs_sum      NUMBER(16,2)
)
tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

--6
create or replace trigger TRIGGER_ZC_P_PRO_BAL_CHG
  after insert or update ON ZC_P_PRO_BAL_CHG
  FOR EACH ROW

BEGIN
  IF (:NEW.STATUS = 'exec') THEN
    delete from zc_p_pro_mitem_bi bi
     where bi.zc_make_code = :NEW.zc_make_code;
  
    
insert into zc_p_pro_mitem_bi 
select zc_make_code,
       zc_bi_no,
       zc_bi_sum,
       zc_bi_jhua_sum,
       zc_bi_do_sum,
       zc_bi_yjba_sum,
       bi_target_code,
       b_acc_code,
       b_acc_name,
       co_code,
       co_name,
       dec_money,
       fund_code,
       fund_name,
       inceptdoc_code,
       inceptdoc_name,
       manage_code,
       manage_name,
       nd,
       org_code,
       org_name,
       origin_code,
       origin_name,
       outlay_code,
       outlay_name,
       payout_code,
       payout_name,
       paytype_code,
       paytype_name,
       project_code,
       project_name,
       project_type_code,
       project_type_name,

 BJD.GONG_HUO_DATE GONG_HUO_DATE,

 where
 BJD.BJ_CODE = BJ.BJ_CODE and BJ.PROJ_CODE = XJ.Proj_Code and
 BJD.XJ_CODE = XJ.XJ_CODE and BJ.STATUS='1';

create or replace view gfmis2014.vw_budget_gb as
select a.sum_id,
       a.avi_money as budget_money,
       a.avi_money - a.use_money - a.minus_money as canuse_money,
       b.en_code,
       b.en_name,
       b.en_id,
       b.mk_code,
       b.mk_name,
       b.mk_id,
       b.bs_code,
       b.bs_name,
       b.bs_id,
       b.bi_code,
       b.bi_name,
       b.bi_id,
       b.pk_code,
       b.pk_name,
       b.pk_id,
       b.bo_code,
       b.bo_name,
       b.bo_id,
       b.mb_code,
       b.mb_name,
       b.mb_id,
       b.bt_code,
       b.bt_name,
       b.bt_id,
       b.bp_code,
       b.bp_name,
       b.bp_id,
       b.bl_code,
       b.bl_name,
       b.bl_id,
       b.bis_code,
       b.bis_name,
       b.bis_id,
       b.sm_code,
       b.sm_name,
       b.sm_id,
       b.gb_code,
       b.gb_name,
       b.gb_id,
       b.saltag_name,
       b.saltag_code,
       b.saltag_id,
       b.file_code,
       b.file_name,
       b.file_id,
       b.budget_vou_code,
       b.budget_vou_name,
       b.budget_vou_id,
       b.gpplan_code,
       b.gpplan_name,
       b.gpplan_id,
       b.inpm_code,
       b.inpm_name,
       b.inpm_id,
       b.set_year,
       a.rg_code
  from gl_balance a, gl_ccids b
 where a.account_id = '{71F7A94B-CE9D-4079-824E-42560832831E}' --单位指标id
   and a.avi_money - a.minus_money - a.use_money >= 0
   and a.ccid = b.ccid
   and a.set_year = b.set_year
   --and a.rg_code = b.rg_code
   --and b.gb_code = '1'   --政府采购标识为是
   --and b.gb_name = '是';

---2
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_WF_ACTION_HISTORY_GK53 AS
(SELECT a.instance_id, a.executor
  FROM wf_action_history a, wf_instance c
 WHERE (a.node_id > -10)
   AND a.instance_id = c.instance_id
   AND c.status > -9   
MINUS
SELECT a.instance_id, a.executor
  FROM wf_current_task a, wf_instance b
 WHERE b.status = 1
   AND a.instance_id = b.instance_id)
   union all
   (SELECT a.instance_id,d.dai_bian_user as executor
FROM wf_action_history a,zc_eb_daibian d,
     wf_instance c
WHERE (a.node_id > -10) AND
      a.instance_id = c.instance_id AND
      c.status>-9      
      and a.executor=d.co_user
MINUS
SELECT a.instance_id, d.dai_bian_user as executor
FROM wf_current_task a,wf_instance b,zc_eb_daibian d
WHERE  b.status = 1 AND
     a.instance_id = b.instance_id
     and a.executor=d.co_user);
---3
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_WF_CURRENT_TASK_ZC_TODO AS
SELECT  a.executor, a.instance_id
   FROM WF_CURRENT_TASK a,WF_INSTANCE b
   WHERE b.STATUS = 1 AND   a.INSTANCE_ID = b.INSTANCE_ID
   AND (A.GK_SEND_STATUS is null or A.GK_SEND_STATUS in ('1','3','4','5','6','7','8','9','10','11'))
union all 
SELECT  d.dai_bian_user as executor, a.instance_id
   FROM WF_CURRENT_TASK a,WF_INSTANCE b,zc_eb_daibian d
   WHERE b.STATUS = 1 AND   a.INSTANCE_ID = b.INSTANCE_ID
   AND (A.GK_SEND_STATUS is null or A.GK_SEND_STATUS in ('1','3','4','5','6','7','8','9','10','11'))
   and a.executor=d.co_user;

--4
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_WF_CURRENT_TASK_ZC_UNTREAD AS
SELECT  a.executor, a.instance_id
FROM WF_CURRENT_TASK a,WF_INSTANCE b
WHERE b.STATUS = 1 AND   a.INSTANCE_ID = b.INSTANCE_ID AND A.GK_SEND_STATUS='2'
union all
SELECT  d.dai_bian_user as executor, a.instance_id
FROM WF_CURRENT_TASK a,WF_INSTANCE b,zc_eb_daibian d
WHERE b.STATUS = 1 AND   a.INSTANCE_ID = b.INSTANCE_ID AND A.GK_SEND_STATUS='2'
and a.executor=d.co_user;

--5
CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_WF_CURRENT_TASK_GK53 AS
SELECT a.executor, a.instance_id
  FROM WF_CURRENT_TASK a, WF_INSTANCE b, wf_node n
 WHERE b.STATUS = 1
   AND a.INSTANCE_ID = b.INSTANCE_ID
   AND (A.GK_SEND_STATUS <> '2' or A.GK_SEND_STATUS is null)
   and n.node_id = a.node_id
   and n.executors_method <> 2
union 
SELECT  d.dai_bian_user as executor, a.instance_id
FROM WF_CURRENT_TASK a,WF_INSTANCE b, wf_node n,zc_eb_daibian d
 WHERE b.STATUS = 1
   AND a.INSTANCE_ID = b.INSTANCE_ID
   AND (A.GK_SEND_STATUS <> '2' or A.GK_SEND_STATUS is null)
   and n.node_id = a.node_id
   and n.executors_method <> 2
   and a.executor=d.co_user
union
select ta.executor, ta.instance_id
  from (SELECT min(CURRENT_TASK_ID) CURRENT_TASK_ID,
               a.instance_id,
               a.node_id
          FROM WF_CURRENT_TASK a, WF_INSTANCE b, wf_node n
         WHERE b.STATUS = 1
           AND a.INSTANCE_ID = b.INSTANCE_ID
           AND (A.GK_SEND_STATUS <> '2' or A.GK_SEND_STATUS is null)
           and n.node_id = a.node_id
           and n.executors_method = 2
         group by a.instance_id, a.node_id) abc,
       WF_CURRENT_TASK ta
 where abc.CURRENT_TASK_ID = ta.current_task_id;

(
  dai_bian_user VARCHAR2(60),
  co_user       VARCHAR2(60),
  co_code       VARCHAR2(60)
)
tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

  is '单位用户';
comment on column ZC_EB_DAIBIAN.co_code
  is '单位编码';

-----------------------20140726----------------------------
--1

    update as_tab_col t set t.is_null='N' where t.tab_id='ZC_FA_CARD' and t.data_item='FA_PURCHASETIME';

--2
create or replace trigger TRIGGER_ZC_P_PRO_BAL_GKBACK_WW
  after update ON ZC_P_PRO_BAL
  FOR EACH ROW
--国库退回时，将状态更新到外网

BEGIN
  IF (:NEW.ZC_BAL_STATUS = 'gkBack') THEN
    delete from zc_data_exchange_redo r where r.record_id = :NEW.ZC_BAL_ID;

    insert into zc_data_exchange_redo
      (id,
       record_name,
       record_id,
       record_content,
       generate_date,
       master_table_name,
       data_type_id,
       data_type_name,
       record_id_col,
       is_exported,
       operate_type)
    values
      (ZC_SEQ_DATA_EXCHANGE_REDO.Nextval,
       '资金支付',
       :NEW.ZC_BAL_ID,
       '',
       SYSDATE(),
       'ZC_P_PRO_BAL',
       'ZC_P_PRO_BAL',
       '资金支付',
       '',
       '0',
       '');

  END IF;
END TRIGGER_ZC_P_PRO_BAL_GKBACK_WW;

(

  zc_bi_do_sum        NUMBER(16,2),

  b_acc_name          VARCHAR2(200),
  co_code             VARCHAR2(60),
  co_name             VARCHAR2(200),
  dec_money           NUMBER(16,2),
  fund_code           VARCHAR2(60),
  fund_name           VARCHAR2(200),
  inceptdoc_code      VARCHAR2(60),
  inceptdoc_name      VARCHAR2(200),
  manage_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  manage_name         VARCHAR2(200),
  nd                  CHAR(4),
  org_code            VARCHAR2(60),
  org_name            VARCHAR2(100),
  origin_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  origin_name         VARCHAR2(200),
  outlay_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  outlay_name         VARCHAR2(200),
  payout_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  payout_name         VARCHAR2(200),
  paytype_code        VARCHAR2(60),
  paytype_name        VARCHAR2(200),
  project_code        VARCHAR2(60),
  project_name        VARCHAR2(200),
  project_type_code   VARCHAR2(60),
  project_type_name   VARCHAR2(200),
  senddoc_code        VARCHAR2(60),
  senddoc_name        VARCHAR2(200),
  senddoc_type_code   VARCHAR2(60),
  senddoc_type_name   VARCHAR2(200),
  zc_cg_type          VARCHAR2(2),
  zc_plan_type        VARCHAR2(2),
  zc_save_num         NUMBER,
  zc_catalogue_code   VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_catalogue_name   VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_year             VARCHAR2(4),
  zc_yep_sum          NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_bi_apd_flag      VARCHAR2(2000),
  zc_fund_remark      VARCHAR2(500),
  zc_fund_file        VARCHAR2(200),
  zc_fund_file_blobid VARCHAR2(200),
  is_add_onfunds      VARCHAR2(4),
  supplement_amount   NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_use_bi_id        VARCHAR2(60),
  gb_name             VARCHAR2(60),
  bt_name             VARCHAR2(60),
  BAL_CHG_ID          VARCHAR2(60)
)

  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

  is '合同代码';

  is '指标编号';

  is '本次使用金额';

  is '需求编号';

  is '已经结算金额';

  is '累计冲红金额';

new:新数据,变更后的数据，这个数据会最终同步到合同指标表中
';

---------------------20141121------------------------------
--1
create or replace procedure sp_zc_yearend_carray (
       makeCodes in varchar2
)
is
       type makeCursorType is ref cursor;
       makeCursor makeCursorType;
       c_make_row zc_p_pro_make%rowtype;

       execSql varchar2(512);
       errors varchar2(256):='';

begin
       execSql := 'select * from zc_p_pro_make where zc_make_code in (' || makeCodes || ')';
       open makeCursor for execSql;
       loop
            fetch makeCursor into c_make_row;
            exit when makeCursor%notfound;

            --调用采购计划结转
            sp_zc_make_yearend_carray(c_make_row.zc_make_code,c_make_row.nd,errors);
            if length(errors) > 0 then
              raise_application_error(-20005,'结转计划时出现问题' || errors );
            end if;

            --调用合同结转
            errors := '';
            sp_zc_ht_yearend_carray(c_make_row.zc_make_code,errors);
            if length(errors) > 0 then
              raise_application_error(-20005,'结转合同时出现问题' || errors);
            end if;


            --调用验收结算结转
            --不结转验收结算数据，在途的数据要求全部走完流程 --20141117 chenjl
           /* errors := '';
            sp_zc_bal_yearend_carray(c_make_row.zc_make_code,errors);
            if length(errors) > 0 then
              raise_application_error(-20005,'结转验收结算时出现问题' || errors);
            end if;*/

            update zc_p_pro_make set zc_yep_flag = '20' where zc_make_code = c_make_row.zc_make_code;
       end loop;
       close makeCursor;

end sp_zc_yearend_carray;


--2
create or replace procedure sp_zc_make_yearend_carray (
       makeCode varchar2,
       nd char,
       errors out varchar2
)
is
       makeTotalSum number:=0;
       balTotalSum number:=0;
       jzTotalSum number:=0;
       jzBiTotalSum number:=0;
       newMakeCode varchar2(128) := makeCode || '_1';

       cursor zcMakeBiCursor is select * from zc_p_pro_mitem_bi where zc_make_code = makeCode and nd = nd; --采购计划资金构成
      makeBiRow zcMakeBiCursor%rowtype;
       biJzSum number:=0;
       newBiSum number:=0;
       errorInfo varchar2(256) := '';
       tempSeq number := 0;


begin
       select nvl(sum(zc_money_bi_sum),0)into  makeTotalSum from  zc_p_pro_make where zc_make_code = makeCode;
       select nvl(sum(zc_bal_sum),0) into balTotalSum from zc_p_pro_bal where zc_make_code = makeCode and zc_bal_status = 'exec'
              and zc_ht_code not in (select zc_ht_code from zc_xmcg_ht where zc_make_code = makeCode and  zc_parht_code is not null);
       select nvl((makeTotalSum - balTotalSum ),0) into jzTotalSum from dual;

       -----------结转采购计划------------------------------------------------------------------------------
      insert into zc_p_pro_make (
              ZC_MAKE_CODE,ZC_MAKE_NAME,CO_CODE,ND,ZC_MAKE_LINKMAN,ZC_MAKE_TEL,ZC_MAKE_STATUS,ZC_INPUT_CODE,ZC_INPUT_DATE,
              ZC_PRO_REMARK,ZC_MONEY_BI_SUM,ZC_MONEY_ZC_SUM,ZC_MAKE_APPR_SNO,ZC_MAKE_APPR,ZC_MAKE_APPR_BLOBID,ZC_REMARK,
              PROCESS_INST_ID,ZC_MAKE_FROM,AGENCY,ZC_IS_AGENCY,ZC_MAKE_ZHAOBIAO,ZC_MAKE_ZHAOBIAO_BLOBID,ZC_MAKE_ZHAOGG,
              ZC_MAKE_ZHAOGG_BLOBID,ZC_MAKE_ZHONGBIAO,ZC_MAKE_ZHONGBIAO_BLOBID,ZC_MAKE_ZHONGGG,ZC_MAKE_ZHONGGG_BLOBID,
              ZC_IS_TO_CGZX,ZC_MAKE_FLAG,ORG_CODE,ZC_PITEM_OPIWAY,ZC_PIFU_CGFS,ZC_PITEM_MODE,ZC_CD_AWDAREA,ZC_IS_ZXQY_ZB,
              ZC_HANGYE_CTG,ORG_NAME,ZC_MONEY_BI_YZX,ZC_MONEY_KY_BGS,ZC_MONEY_BG_ZXS,ZC_FGKZBFS_SMWJ_BLOBID,ZC_FGKZBFS_SMWJ,
              AGENCY_NAME,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA,ZC_MONEY_HT_YBA,ZC_FUKUAN_TYPE,ZC_WEITO_DATE,ZC_YEP_FLAG,ZC_YEP_SUM,ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,
              ZC_PROJ_ORIGN,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA_ZJ,ZC_IS_NOTARY,ZC_IS_IMP,ZC_IS_REMARK,ZC_IMP_FILE,ZC_IMP_FILE_BLOBID,ZC_PRINT_STATUS,
              ZC_MAKE_SEQUENCE, ZC_IS_BUDGET,ZC_XIEYI_END_DATE,ZC_NO_SHIP_REASON,ZC_ATTR1,ZC_ATTR2,ZC_ATTR3,ZC_ATTR4,ZC_ATTR5,
              ZC_TEMP_MAKE_CODE
       )
       select
              newMakeCode,ZC_MAKE_NAME,CO_CODE,ND+1,ZC_MAKE_LINKMAN,ZC_MAKE_TEL,ZC_MAKE_STATUS,ZC_INPUT_CODE,ZC_INPUT_DATE,
              ZC_PRO_REMARK,jzTotalSum,ZC_MONEY_ZC_SUM,ZC_MAKE_APPR_SNO,ZC_MAKE_APPR,ZC_MAKE_APPR_BLOBID,ZC_REMARK,
              PROCESS_INST_ID,ZC_MAKE_FROM,AGENCY,ZC_IS_AGENCY,ZC_MAKE_ZHAOBIAO,ZC_MAKE_ZHAOBIAO_BLOBID,ZC_MAKE_ZHAOGG,
              ZC_MAKE_ZHAOGG_BLOBID,ZC_MAKE_ZHONGBIAO,ZC_MAKE_ZHONGBIAO_BLOBID,ZC_MAKE_ZHONGGG,ZC_MAKE_ZHONGGG_BLOBID,
              ZC_IS_TO_CGZX,ZC_MAKE_FLAG,ORG_CODE,ZC_PITEM_OPIWAY,ZC_PIFU_CGFS,ZC_PITEM_MODE,ZC_CD_AWDAREA,ZC_IS_ZXQY_ZB,
              ZC_HANGYE_CTG,ORG_NAME,ZC_MONEY_BI_YZX,ZC_MONEY_KY_BGS,ZC_MONEY_BG_ZXS,ZC_FGKZBFS_SMWJ_BLOBID,ZC_FGKZBFS_SMWJ,
              AGENCY_NAME,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA,ZC_MONEY_HT_YBA,ZC_FUKUAN_TYPE,ZC_WEITO_DATE,'00',0,ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,
              ZC_PROJ_ORIGN,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA_ZJ,ZC_IS_NOTARY,ZC_IS_IMP,ZC_IS_REMARK,ZC_IMP_FILE,ZC_IMP_FILE_BLOBID,ZC_PRINT_STATUS,
              ZC_MAKE_SEQUENCE, ZC_IS_BUDGET,ZC_XIEYI_END_DATE,ZC_NO_SHIP_REASON,ZC_ATTR1,ZC_ATTR2,ZC_ATTR3,ZC_ATTR4,ZC_ATTR5,
              ZC_TEMP_MAKE_CODE
        from zc_p_pro_make where zc_make_code = makeCode;

        --结转商品明细
        insert into zc_p_pro_mitem (
                  ZC_PITEM_CODE,ZC_MAKE_CODE,ZC_YEAR,ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,ZC_PITEM_NAME,ZC_PITEM_ARR_DATE,
                  ZC_BASE_GGYQ,ZC_PITEM_ATTACH,ZC_PITEM_ATTACH_BLOBID,ZC_PINMU_CTLG,ZC_MAKE_NEW_CODE,ZC_CAIG_NUM,
                  ZC_ITEM_SUM,ZC_MER_PRICE,BUDGET_BI_MONEY,BUDGET_OTHER_MONEY,ZC_BRA_CODE,ZC_MER_CODE,ZC_SU_CODE,
                  ZC_IS_SU_JIN_JIA,ZC_IS_CHENG_JIAO,ZC_JIN_JIA_SUBMIT_DATE,ZC_IS_GONG_HUO,ZC_NO_GONG_HUO_REASON
                 )
        select
                ZC_PITEM_CODE,newMakeCode,ZC_YEAR+1,ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,ZC_PITEM_NAME,ZC_PITEM_ARR_DATE,
                ZC_BASE_GGYQ,ZC_PITEM_ATTACH,ZC_PITEM_ATTACH_BLOBID,ZC_PINMU_CTLG,ZC_MAKE_NEW_CODE,0,
                0,0,BUDGET_BI_MONEY,BUDGET_OTHER_MONEY,ZC_BRA_CODE,ZC_MER_CODE,ZC_SU_CODE,
                ZC_IS_SU_JIN_JIA,ZC_IS_CHENG_JIAO,ZC_JIN_JIA_SUBMIT_DATE,ZC_IS_GONG_HUO,ZC_NO_GONG_HUO_REASON
        from zc_p_pro_mitem where zc_make_code = makeCode;

exception
  when others then
    errors := errors || '结转采购计划时出错。';
    raise_application_error(-20005,errors);
end sp_zc_make_yearend_carray;

--3
create or replace procedure sp_zc_ht_yearend_carray(
       makeCode varchar2,
       errors out varchar2
)
is
       cursor htCursor is select * from zc_xmcg_ht where zc_make_code = makeCode and zc_ht_status <> 'cancel' and zc_parht_code is null;
       htRow htCursor%rowtype;
       htBalExecSum number := 0; -- 合同对应终审验收结算总金额
       htJzSum number := 0; --合同结转金额
       htBiJzSum number := 0; -- 合同资金结转金额
       htBiExecSum number := 0; -- 已经执行完成的资金总金额
       newHtCode varchar2(128);
       newMakeCode varchar2(128);

       cursor htBiCursor(zchtCodeTemp varchar2) is select * from zc_xmcg_ht_bi where zc_ht_code = zchtCodeTemp;
       htBiRow htBiCursor%rowtype;
begin
       newMakeCode := makeCode || '_1';
       open htCursor;
            loop
              fetch htCursor into htRow;
              exit when htCursor%notfound;
              select nvl(sum(zc_bal_sum),0) into htBalExecSum from zc_p_pro_bal where zc_ht_code = htRow.Zc_Ht_Code and zc_bal_status = 'exec';
              if htRow.Zc_Ht_Num > htBalExecSum then
                newHtCode := htRow.Zc_Ht_Code || '_1';
                htJzSum := htRow.Zc_Ht_Num - htBalExecSum;
                --结转合同主表
                insert into zc_xmcg_ht (
                      ZC_HT_CODE,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA,ZC_HT_NAME,ZC_HT_TYPE,ZC_REQ_CODE,ZC_MAKE_CODE,ZC_BID_CODE,CO_CODE,ND,
                      ZC_SGN_DATE,ZC_SU_NAME,ZC_JCKDL_MC,ZC_HT_NUM,ZC_CZ_LEVEL,ZC_FUKUAN_TYPE,ZC_FUKUAN_YUED,ZC_CHECK_TYPE,
                      ZC_CON_TEXT,ZC_CON_TEXT_BLOBID,ZC_HT_STATUS,ZC_AGEY_CODE,ZC_ZG_CS_CODE,ZC_SM_PJ1,ZC_SM_PJ2,ZC_SM_PJ3,
                      ZC_SM_PJ4,EXECUTOR,EXECUTE_DATE,PROCESS_INST_ID,ZC_PARHT_CODE,ZC_SU_CODE,ZC_SU_ACC_CODE,ZC_SU_BANK_CODE,
                      ZC_SU_BANK_NAME,ZC_SU_TEL,ZC_SU_LINKMAN,ZC_IS_ZXQY_ZB,ZC_GNW,ZC_SNW,ZC_ARRIVE_ADDR,ZC_ARRIVE_DATE,
                      ZC_HANGYE_CTG,ZC_SK_REN,ZC_ZB_NAME,ZC_ZB_CODE,ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,ZC_ISREWRITE,ZC_CG_LEIXING,ZC_ZG_CS_NAME,
                      ZC_BGSP_BH,ZC_DELIVERY_EVL,ZC_PRICE_EVL,ZC_QUANTITY_EVL,ZC_SERVICE_EVL,ZC_MEMO,ZC_BID_CONTENT,
                      ZC_DELIVERY_DATE,ZC_DELIVERY_ADDR,ZC_DELIVERY_TYPE,AGENCY,ORG_CODE
                )
                select
                        newHtCode,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA,ZC_HT_NAME,ZC_HT_TYPE,newMakeCode,newMakeCode,ZC_BID_CODE,CO_CODE,ND+1,
                        ZC_SGN_DATE,ZC_SU_NAME,ZC_JCKDL_MC,htJzSum,ZC_CZ_LEVEL,ZC_FUKUAN_TYPE,ZC_FUKUAN_YUED,ZC_CHECK_TYPE,
                        ZC_CON_TEXT,ZC_CON_TEXT_BLOBID,ZC_HT_STATUS,ZC_AGEY_CODE,ZC_ZG_CS_CODE,ZC_SM_PJ1,ZC_SM_PJ2,ZC_SM_PJ3,
                        ZC_SM_PJ4,EXECUTOR,EXECUTE_DATE,PROCESS_INST_ID,ZC_PARHT_CODE,ZC_SU_CODE,ZC_SU_ACC_CODE,ZC_SU_BANK_CODE,
                        ZC_SU_BANK_NAME,ZC_SU_TEL,ZC_SU_LINKMAN,ZC_IS_ZXQY_ZB,ZC_GNW,ZC_SNW,ZC_ARRIVE_ADDR,ZC_ARRIVE_DATE,
                        ZC_HANGYE_CTG,ZC_SK_REN,ZC_ZB_NAME,ZC_ZB_CODE,ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,ZC_ISREWRITE,ZC_CG_LEIXING,ZC_ZG_CS_NAME,
                        ZC_BGSP_BH,ZC_DELIVERY_EVL,ZC_PRICE_EVL,ZC_QUANTITY_EVL,ZC_SERVICE_EVL,ZC_MEMO,ZC_BID_CONTENT,
                        ZC_DELIVERY_DATE,ZC_DELIVERY_ADDR,ZC_DELIVERY_TYPE,AGENCY,ORG_CODE
                from zc_xmcg_ht where zc_ht_code = htRow.Zc_Ht_Code;

               

                --结转商品明细
                insert into ZC_T_BCHT_ITEM (
                      ZC_HT_CODE,ZC_CTGRY_ID,ZC_YEAR,ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,ZC_IS_JNJS,ZC_BRA_NAME,
                      ZC_MER_SPEC,ZC_ITEM_VAL,ZC_CAIG_SHL,ZC_SP_NAME,ZC_MER_IS_ZZCX,ZC_MER_IS_LSHB,ZC_MER_M_PRICE,
                      ZC_HT_BI_MONEY,ZC_HT_OTHER_MONEY,ZC_HT_GK_MONEY,ZC_ITEM_SUM,BUDGET_BI_MONEY,BUDGET_OTHER_MONEY,
                      ZC_CAIG_JLDW,ZC_CAIG_PRICE,ZC_CAIG_MONEY
                      )
                select newHtCode,ZC_CTGRY_ID,ZC_YEAR+1,ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,ZC_IS_JNJS,ZC_BRA_NAME,
                        ZC_MER_SPEC,ZC_ITEM_VAL,ZC_CAIG_SHL,ZC_SP_NAME,ZC_MER_IS_ZZCX,ZC_MER_IS_LSHB,ZC_MER_M_PRICE,
                        ZC_HT_BI_MONEY,ZC_HT_OTHER_MONEY,ZC_HT_GK_MONEY,ZC_ITEM_SUM,BUDGET_BI_MONEY,BUDGET_OTHER_MONEY,
                        ZC_CAIG_JLDW,ZC_CAIG_PRICE,ZC_CAIG_MONEY
                from ZC_T_BCHT_ITEM where zc_ht_code = htRow.Zc_Ht_Code;

              end if;
            end loop;
       close htCursor;
exception
  when others then
    errors := '结转合同出现问题';
    raise_application_error(-20005,'结转合同出现问题');
end sp_zc_ht_yearend_carray;

-- Create table
create table ZC_P_PRO_MAKE_SUPPLEMENT
(
  zc_supplement_code   VARCHAR2(30) not null,
  zc_make_code         VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_supplement_status VARCHAR2(5),
  process_inst_id      NUMBER,
  add_money            NUMBER(16,2),
  zc_input_name        VARCHAR2(60),
  zc_input_code        VARCHAR2(30),
  zc_input_date        DATE,
  zc_remark            VARCHAR2(200),
  co_code              VARCHAR2(30),
  nd                   CHAR(4)
)
tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );
-- Add comments to the table 
comment on table ZC_P_PRO_MAKE_SUPPLEMENT
  is '追加资金';
-- Add comments to the columns 
comment on column ZC_P_PRO_MAKE_SUPPLEMENT.add_money
  is '本次追加金额';
comment on column ZC_P_PRO_MAKE_SUPPLEMENT.zc_input_name
  is '录入人姓名';
comment on column ZC_P_PRO_MAKE_SUPPLEMENT.zc_input_code
  is '录入人代码';
comment on column ZC_P_PRO_MAKE_SUPPLEMENT.zc_input_date
  is '录入时间';
comment on column ZC_P_PRO_MAKE_SUPPLEMENT.zc_remark
  is '备注';
-- Create/Recreate primary, unique and foreign key constraints 
alter table ZC_P_PRO_MAKE_SUPPLEMENT
  add constraint ZC_SUPPLEMENT_PK primary key (ZC_SUPPLEMENT_CODE)
  using index 
  tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 2
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

alter table ZC_P_PRO_BAL_BI add zc_bal_bi_id VARCHAR2(60);

  is '采购计划编号';
comment on column ZC_P_PRO_BAL_BI.zc_bal_bi_id
  is '这个表的主键，原不需要，后有了追加资金，以前的复合主键不够了，增加这个字段，参与到符合主键中';

--3
-- Create sequence 
create sequence SEQ_ZcProBalBiId
minvalue 1
maxvalue 9999999999
start with 1
cache 5;

create table zc_p_pro_bal_bi2 as select * from zc_p_pro_bal_bi where 1!=1;

insert into zc_p_pro_bal_bi2
  (zc_bal_id, zc_bi_no, zc_bi_bcjs_sum, zc_code, zc_am_billno, zc_am_status, zc_ht_code, zc_bi_yjjs_sum, zc_bi_chba_sum, bal_mode_code, outlay_code, zc_fund_code, zc_origin_code, zc_bi_sum, zc_ht_bi_no, zc_send_date, zc_fund_name, zc_origin_name, zc_paytype_code, zc_paytype_name, zc_bi_bcsy_sum, zc_catalogue_code, zc_catalogue_name, zc_bis_code, zc_bis_name, zc_b_acc_code, zc_b_acc_name, outlay_name, out_lay_is_leaf, zc_bal_bi_id)

select zc_bal_id, zc_bi_no, zc_bi_bcjs_sum, zc_code, zc_am_billno, zc_am_status, zc_ht_code, zc_bi_yjjs_sum, zc_bi_chba_sum, bal_mode_code, outlay_code, zc_fund_code, zc_origin_code, zc_bi_sum, zc_ht_bi_no, zc_send_date, zc_fund_name, zc_origin_name, zc_paytype_code, zc_paytype_name, zc_bi_bcsy_sum, zc_catalogue_code, zc_catalogue_name, zc_bis_code, zc_bis_name, zc_b_acc_code, zc_b_acc_name, outlay_name, out_lay_is_leaf, SEQ_ZcProBalBiId.Nextval 
from zc_p_pro_bal_bi
;

  add constraint ZC_P_PRO_BAL_BI_pk primary key (ZC_BAL_BI_ID);
  
--5
create or replace procedure sp_zc_ht_yearend_carray(
       makeCode varchar2,
       errors out varchar2
)
is
       cursor htCursor is select * from zc_xmcg_ht where zc_make_code = makeCode and zc_ht_status <> 'cancel' ;
       htRow htCursor%rowtype;
       htBalExecSum number := 0; -- 合同对应终审验收结算总金额
       htJzSum number := 0; --合同结转金额
       htBiJzSum number := 0; -- 合同资金结转金额
       htBiExecSum number := 0; -- 已经执行完成的资金总金额
       newHtCode varchar2(128);
       newMakeCode varchar2(128);

       cursor htBiCursor(zchtCodeTemp varchar2) is select * from zc_xmcg_ht_bi where zc_ht_code = zchtCodeTemp;
       htBiRow htBiCursor%rowtype;
begin
       newMakeCode := makeCode || '_1';
       open htCursor;
            loop
              fetch htCursor into htRow;
              exit when htCursor%notfound;
              select nvl(sum(zc_bal_sum),0) into htBalExecSum from zc_p_pro_bal where zc_ht_code = htRow.Zc_Ht_Code and zc_bal_status = 'exec';
              if htRow.Zc_Ht_Num > htBalExecSum then
                newHtCode := htRow.Zc_Ht_Code || '_1';
                htJzSum := htRow.Zc_Ht_Num - htBalExecSum;
                --结转合同主表
                insert into zc_xmcg_ht (
                      ZC_HT_CODE,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA,ZC_HT_NAME,ZC_HT_TYPE,ZC_REQ_CODE,ZC_MAKE_CODE,ZC_BID_CODE,CO_CODE,ND,
                      ZC_SGN_DATE,ZC_SU_NAME,ZC_JCKDL_MC,ZC_HT_NUM,ZC_CZ_LEVEL,ZC_FUKUAN_TYPE,ZC_FUKUAN_YUED,ZC_CHECK_TYPE,
                      ZC_CON_TEXT,ZC_CON_TEXT_BLOBID,ZC_HT_STATUS,ZC_AGEY_CODE,ZC_ZG_CS_CODE,ZC_SM_PJ1,ZC_SM_PJ2,ZC_SM_PJ3,
                      ZC_SM_PJ4,EXECUTOR,EXECUTE_DATE,PROCESS_INST_ID,ZC_PARHT_CODE,ZC_SU_CODE,ZC_SU_ACC_CODE,ZC_SU_BANK_CODE,
                      ZC_SU_BANK_NAME,ZC_SU_TEL,ZC_SU_LINKMAN,ZC_IS_ZXQY_ZB,ZC_GNW,ZC_SNW,ZC_ARRIVE_ADDR,ZC_ARRIVE_DATE,
                      ZC_HANGYE_CTG,ZC_SK_REN,ZC_ZB_NAME,ZC_ZB_CODE,ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,ZC_ISREWRITE,ZC_CG_LEIXING,ZC_ZG_CS_NAME,
                      ZC_BGSP_BH,ZC_DELIVERY_EVL,ZC_PRICE_EVL,ZC_QUANTITY_EVL,ZC_SERVICE_EVL,ZC_MEMO,ZC_BID_CONTENT,
                      ZC_DELIVERY_DATE,ZC_DELIVERY_ADDR,ZC_DELIVERY_TYPE,AGENCY,ORG_CODE
                )
                select
                        newHtCode,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA,ZC_HT_NAME,ZC_HT_TYPE,newMakeCode,newMakeCode,ZC_BID_CODE,CO_CODE,ND+1,
                        ZC_SGN_DATE,ZC_SU_NAME,ZC_JCKDL_MC,htJzSum,ZC_CZ_LEVEL,ZC_FUKUAN_TYPE,ZC_FUKUAN_YUED,ZC_CHECK_TYPE,
                        ZC_CON_TEXT,ZC_CON_TEXT_BLOBID,ZC_HT_STATUS,ZC_AGEY_CODE,ZC_ZG_CS_CODE,ZC_SM_PJ1,ZC_SM_PJ2,ZC_SM_PJ3,
                        ZC_SM_PJ4,EXECUTOR,EXECUTE_DATE,PROCESS_INST_ID,ZC_PARHT_CODE,ZC_SU_CODE,ZC_SU_ACC_CODE,ZC_SU_BANK_CODE,
                        ZC_SU_BANK_NAME,ZC_SU_TEL,ZC_SU_LINKMAN,ZC_IS_ZXQY_ZB,ZC_GNW,ZC_SNW,ZC_ARRIVE_ADDR,ZC_ARRIVE_DATE,
                        ZC_HANGYE_CTG,ZC_SK_REN,ZC_ZB_NAME,ZC_ZB_CODE,ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,ZC_ISREWRITE,ZC_CG_LEIXING,ZC_ZG_CS_NAME,
                        ZC_BGSP_BH,ZC_DELIVERY_EVL,ZC_PRICE_EVL,ZC_QUANTITY_EVL,ZC_SERVICE_EVL,ZC_MEMO,ZC_BID_CONTENT,
                        ZC_DELIVERY_DATE,ZC_DELIVERY_ADDR,ZC_DELIVERY_TYPE,AGENCY,ORG_CODE
                from zc_xmcg_ht where zc_ht_code = htRow.Zc_Ht_Code;



                --结转商品明细
                insert into ZC_T_BCHT_ITEM (
                      ZC_HT_CODE,ZC_CTGRY_ID,ZC_YEAR,ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,ZC_IS_JNJS,ZC_BRA_NAME,
                      ZC_MER_SPEC,ZC_ITEM_VAL,ZC_CAIG_SHL,ZC_SP_NAME,ZC_MER_IS_ZZCX,ZC_MER_IS_LSHB,ZC_MER_M_PRICE,
                      ZC_HT_BI_MONEY,ZC_HT_OTHER_MONEY,ZC_HT_GK_MONEY,ZC_ITEM_SUM,BUDGET_BI_MONEY,BUDGET_OTHER_MONEY,
                      ZC_CAIG_JLDW,ZC_CAIG_PRICE,ZC_CAIG_MONEY
                      )
                select newHtCode,ZC_CTGRY_ID,ZC_YEAR+1,ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,ZC_IS_JNJS,ZC_BRA_NAME,
                        ZC_MER_SPEC,ZC_ITEM_VAL,ZC_CAIG_SHL,ZC_SP_NAME,ZC_MER_IS_ZZCX,ZC_MER_IS_LSHB,ZC_MER_M_PRICE,
                        ZC_HT_BI_MONEY,ZC_HT_OTHER_MONEY,ZC_HT_GK_MONEY,ZC_ITEM_SUM,BUDGET_BI_MONEY,BUDGET_OTHER_MONEY,
                        ZC_CAIG_JLDW,ZC_CAIG_PRICE,ZC_CAIG_MONEY
                from ZC_T_BCHT_ITEM where zc_ht_code = htRow.Zc_Ht_Code;

              end if;
            end loop;
       close htCursor;
exception
  when others then
    errors := '结转合同出现问题';
    raise_application_error(-20005,'结转合同出现问题');
end sp_zc_ht_yearend_carray;

       htBiExecSum number := 0; -- 已经执行完成的资金总金额

       newMakeCode varchar2(128);

                      ZC_SM_PJ4,EXECUTOR,EXECUTE_DATE,PROCESS_INST_ID,ZC_PARHT_CODE,ZC_SU_CODE,ZC_SU_ACC_CODE,ZC_SU_BANK_CODE,
                      ZC_SU_BANK_NAME,ZC_SU_TEL,ZC_SU_LINKMAN,ZC_IS_ZXQY_ZB,ZC_GNW,ZC_SNW,ZC_ARRIVE_ADDR,ZC_ARRIVE_DATE,
                      ZC_HANGYE_CTG,ZC_SK_REN,ZC_ZB_NAME,ZC_ZB_CODE,ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,ZC_ISREWRITE,ZC_CG_LEIXING,ZC_ZG_CS_NAME,

                      ZC_DELIVERY_DATE,ZC_DELIVERY_ADDR,ZC_DELIVERY_TYPE,AGENCY,ORG_CODE,is_zi_chan
                )
                select
                        newHtCode,ZC_DIYU_DAIMA,ZC_HT_NAME,ZC_HT_TYPE,newMakeCode,newMakeCode,ZC_BID_CODE,CO_CODE,ND+1,
                        ZC_SGN_DATE,ZC_SU_NAME,ZC_JCKDL_MC,htJzSum,ZC_CZ_LEVEL,ZC_FUKUAN_TYPE,ZC_FUKUAN_YUED,ZC_CHECK_TYPE,
                        ZC_CON_TEXT,ZC_CON_TEXT_BLOBID,ZC_HT_STATUS,ZC_AGEY_CODE,ZC_ZG_CS_CODE,ZC_SM_PJ1,ZC_SM_PJ2,ZC_SM_PJ3,
                        ZC_SM_PJ4,EXECUTOR,EXECUTE_DATE,PROCESS_INST_ID,ZC_PARHT_CODE,ZC_SU_CODE,ZC_SU_ACC_CODE,ZC_SU_BANK_CODE,
                        ZC_SU_BANK_NAME,ZC_SU_TEL,ZC_SU_LINKMAN,ZC_IS_ZXQY_ZB,ZC_GNW,ZC_SNW,ZC_ARRIVE_ADDR,ZC_ARRIVE_DATE,
                        ZC_HANGYE_CTG,ZC_SK_REN,ZC_ZB_NAME,ZC_ZB_CODE,ZC_BI_NZJZ_SUM,ZC_ISREWRITE,ZC_CG_LEIXING,ZC_ZG_CS_NAME,
                        ZC_BGSP_BH,ZC_DELIVERY_EVL,ZC_PRICE_EVL,ZC_QUANTITY_EVL,ZC_SERVICE_EVL,ZC_MEMO,ZC_BID_CONTENT,
                        ZC_DELIVERY_DATE,ZC_DELIVERY_ADDR,ZC_DELIVERY_TYPE,AGENCY,ORG_CODE,is_zi_chan
                from zc_xmcg_ht where zc_ht_code = htRow.Zc_Ht_Code;



                --结转商品明细
                insert into ZC_T_BCHT_ITEM (
                      ZC_HT_CODE,ZC_CTGRY_ID,ZC_YEAR,ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,ZC_IS_JNJS,ZC_BRA_NAME,
                      ZC_MER_SPEC,ZC_ITEM_VAL,ZC_CAIG_SHL,ZC_SP_NAME,ZC_MER_IS_ZZCX,ZC_MER_IS_LSHB,ZC_MER_M_PRICE,
                      ZC_HT_BI_MONEY,ZC_HT_OTHER_MONEY,ZC_HT_GK_MONEY,ZC_ITEM_SUM,BUDGET_BI_MONEY,BUDGET_OTHER_MONEY,
                      ZC_CAIG_JLDW,ZC_CAIG_PRICE,ZC_CAIG_MONEY
                      )
                select newHtCode,ZC_CTGRY_ID,ZC_YEAR+1,ZC_CATALOGUE_CODE,ZC_CATALOGUE_NAME,ZC_IS_JNJS,ZC_BRA_NAME,
                        ZC_MER_SPEC,ZC_ITEM_VAL,ZC_CAIG_SHL,ZC_SP_NAME,ZC_MER_IS_ZZCX,ZC_MER_IS_LSHB,ZC_MER_M_PRICE,
                        ZC_HT_BI_MONEY,ZC_HT_OTHER_MONEY,ZC_HT_GK_MONEY,ZC_ITEM_SUM,BUDGET_BI_MONEY,BUDGET_OTHER_MONEY,
                        ZC_CAIG_JLDW,ZC_CAIG_PRICE,ZC_CAIG_MONEY
                from ZC_T_BCHT_ITEM where zc_ht_code = htRow.Zc_Ht_Code;

              end if;
            end loop;
       close htCursor;
exception
  when others then
    errors := '结转合同出现问题';
    raise_application_error(-20005,'结转合同出现问题');
end sp_zc_ht_yearend_carray;

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW V_ZC_XUNJIA_OPEN_BID AS
SELECT P.PROJ_CODE PROJ_CODE,
       P.PROJ_NAME PROJ_NAME,
       K.PACK_CODE PACK_CODE,
       K.PACK_NAME PACK_NAME,
       K.PACK_BUDGET PACK_BUDGET,
       '0' STATUS,
       P.Attn MANAGER_CODE,
       P.ND ND,
       RFQ.OPEN_BID_REMARK,
       PLAN.OPEN_BID_TIME OPEN_BID_DATE,
       '0' OPEN_BID_STATUS,
       NULL PROCESS_INST_ID,
       NULL WIN_BID_PROVIDER_NAME,
       NULL WIN_BID_PROVIDER_CODE,
       NULL WIN_BID_SUM,
       PLAN.Open_Bid_Time RE_OPEN_BID_DATE,
       PLAN.SELL_START_TIME,
       PLAN.SELL_END_TIME,
       PLAN.BID_END_TIME,
       PLAN.PLAN_CODE,
       '' RFQ_CODE,
       NULL CREATE_DATE,
       P.Attn_Name CREATOR,
       NULL RFQ_TEAM_OPINION,
       '' BUZHANG_OPINION,
       '' ZHUREN_OPINION,
       NULL REASON,
       0 IS_GOON_AUDIT,
       NULL ORG_CODE,
       P.AGENCY,
       k.pack_max_price,
       K.CO_CODE --采购单位编号
  FROM ZC_EB_PROJ        P,
       ZC_EB_PACK        K,
       v_ZC_EB_pack_PLAN PLAN,
       ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK    RFQ
 WHERE P.PROJ_CODE = K.PROJ_CODE
   AND PLAN.PROJ_CODE = k.PROJ_CODE
   and plan.pack_code = k.pack_code
   AND K.PACK_CODE = RFQ.PACK_CODE(+)
   and k.proj_code = RFQ.Proj_Code(+)
   AND PLAN.OPEN_BID_TIME <= SYSDATE
   AND (RFQ.PACK_CODE IS NULL) --延期的项目到了开标时间，也让选择出来。
   AND P.PUR_TYPE = '5'
   AND P.STATUS = 'exec'
 UNION
 SELECT ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.PROJ_CODE PROJ_CODE,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.PROJ_NAME PROJ_NAME,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.PACK_CODE PACK_CODE,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.PACK_NAME PACK_NAME,
        ZC_EB_PACK.PACK_BUDGET PACK_BUDGET,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.STATUS STATUS,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.MANAGER_CODE MANAGER_CODE,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.ND ND,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. OPEN_BID_REMARK,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.OPEN_BID_DATE OPEN_BID_DATE,
        case
          when ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.RE_OPEN_BID_DATE < sysdate and
               ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.Open_Bid_Status = '2' then
           '0'
          else
           ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.Open_Bid_Status
        end as Open_Bid_Status,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. PROCESS_INST_ID,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. WIN_BID_PROVIDER_NAME,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. WIN_BID_PROVIDER_CODE,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. WIN_BID_SUM,
        PLAN.open_bid_time OPEN_BID_DATE,
        PLAN.SELL_START_TIME,
        PLAN.SELL_END_TIME,
        PLAN.BID_END_TIME,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.PLAN_CODE,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. RFQ_CODE,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. CREATE_DATE,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.CREATOR,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. RFQ_TEAM_OPINION,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.BUZHANG_OPINION,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK. ZHUREN_OPINION,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.REASON,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.IS_GOON_AUDIT,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.ORG_CODE,
        ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.AGENCY,
        ZC_EB_PACK.pack_max_price,
        ZC_EB_PACK.CO_CODE --采购单位编号
   FROM ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK    ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK,
        ZC_EB_PACK        ZC_EB_PACK,
        v_ZC_EB_pack_PLAN PLAN
  WHERE ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.PACK_CODE = ZC_EB_PACK.PACK_CODE
    and ZC_EB_RFQ_PACK.Proj_Code = ZC_EB_PACK.Proj_Code
    and ZC_EB_PACK.Proj_Code = plan.proj_code
    and ZC_EB_PACK.Pack_Code = plan.pack_code;

CREATE TABLE ZC_BRAND
(
	BRAND_NAME           VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	BRAND_CODE           VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,
	LINK_MAN             VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	LINK_TEL             VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	LINK_MOBILE          VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	LINK_FAX             VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	LINK_ADDRESS         VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	IS_ENABLE            CHAR(18) NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_BRAND IS '品牌';



CREATE UNIQUE INDEX XPKZCBRAND ON ZC_BRAND
(BRAND_CODE   ASC);



ALTER TABLE ZC_BRAND
	ADD CONSTRAINT  XPKZCBRAND PRIMARY KEY (BRAND_CODE);



CREATE TABLE ZC_GOODS
(
	BRAND_CODE           VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	GOODS_CODE           VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,
	GOODS_NAME           VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	IS_ENABLE            CHAR(18) NULL ,
	PRICE_MAKET          INTEGER NULL ,
	PRICE_XY             INTEGER NULL ,
	SPEC1                VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	SPEC2                VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	SPEC3                VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	SPEC4                VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	SPEC5                VARCHAR2(20) NULL ,
	SPEC6                VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	SPEC7                VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	SPEC8                VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	SPEC9                VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	GOODS_CATALOG_CODE   VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	thumbnail_ID         VARCHAR2(50) NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_GOODS IS '商品';



CREATE UNIQUE INDEX XPKZCGOODS ON ZC_GOODS
(GOODS_CODE   ASC);



ALTER TABLE ZC_GOODS
	ADD CONSTRAINT  XPKZCGOODS PRIMARY KEY (GOODS_CODE);



CREATE TABLE ZC_GOODS_CATA_TO_BRAND
(
	BRAND_CODE           VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	GOODS_CATALOG_CODE   VARCHAR2(50) NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_GOODS_CATA_TO_BRAND IS '商品目录与品牌';



CREATE TABLE ZC_GOODS_CATA_TO_CATA
(
	zc_year              CHAR(4) NULL ,
	zc_catalogue_code    VARCHAR2(30) NULL ,
	GOODS_CATALOG_CODE   VARCHAR2(50) NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_GOODS_CATA_TO_CATA IS '商品目录与品目';




COMMENT ON COLUMN ZC_GOODS_CATA_TO_CATA.zc_year IS '品目年度';




COMMENT ON COLUMN ZC_GOODS_CATA_TO_CATA.zc_catalogue_code IS '品目代码';



CREATE TABLE ZC_GOODS_CATALOG
(
	GOODS_CATALOG_CODE   VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,
	GOODS_CATALOG_NAME   VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	SHOW_INDEX           INTEGER NULL ,
	SPEC_CODE            VARCHAR2(50) NULL ,
	IS_ENABLE            CHAR(18) NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_GOODS_CATALOG IS '商品目录';



CREATE UNIQUE INDEX XPKZCGOODSCATALOG ON ZC_GOODS_CATALOG
(GOODS_CATALOG_CODE   ASC);



ALTER TABLE ZC_GOODS_CATALOG
	ADD CONSTRAINT  XPKZCGOODSCATALOG PRIMARY KEY (GOODS_CATALOG_CODE);



CREATE TABLE ZC_GOODS_IMAGE
(
	GOODS_CODE           VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,
	IMAGE_ID             VARCHAR2(50) NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_GOODS_IMAGE IS '商品图片';



CREATE UNIQUE INDEX XPKZCGOODSIMAGE ON ZC_GOODS_IMAGE
(GOODS_CODE   ASC);



ALTER TABLE ZC_GOODS_IMAGE
	ADD CONSTRAINT  XPKZCGOODSIMAGE PRIMARY KEY (GOODS_CODE);



CREATE TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC
(
	GOODS_CODE           VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,
	SPEC_CODE            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,
	SPEC                 VARCHAR2(100) NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC IS '商品信息';



CREATE UNIQUE INDEX XPKZCGOODSSPEC ON ZC_GOODS_SPEC
(GOODS_CODE   ASC,SPEC_CODE   ASC);



ALTER TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC
	ADD CONSTRAINT  XPKZCGOODSSPEC PRIMARY KEY (GOODS_CODE,SPEC_CODE);



CREATE TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC_LONG
(
	GOODS_CODE           VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,
	SPEC_CODE            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,
	SPEC_LONG            CLOB NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC_LONG IS '商品长文本信息';



CREATE UNIQUE INDEX XPKZCGOODSSPECLONG ON ZC_GOODS_SPEC_LONG
(GOODS_CODE   ASC,SPEC_CODE   ASC);



ALTER TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC_LONG
	ADD CONSTRAINT  XPKZCGOODSSPECLONG PRIMARY KEY (GOODS_CODE,SPEC_CODE);



CREATE TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC_TEMPLATE
(
	SPEC_CODE            VARCHAR2(50) NOT NULL ,

	SPEC_IS_SIMPLE_SHOW  CHAR(18) NULL ,
	SPEC_SIMPLE_SHOW_INDEX INTEGER NULL ,
	IS_LONG_TXT          CHAR(18) NULL ,
	IS_ENABLE            CHAR(18) NULL 
);



COMMENT ON TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC_TEMPLATE IS '商品规格参数模板';



CREATE UNIQUE INDEX XPKGOODSTEMPLATE ON ZC_GOODS_SPEC_TEMPLATE
(SPEC_CODE   ASC);



ALTER TABLE ZC_GOODS_SPEC_TEMPLATE
	ADD CONSTRAINT  XPKGOODSTEMPLATE PRIMARY KEY (SPEC_CODE);

-- Create table
create table ZC_DINGDIAN
(
  dd_code             VARCHAR2(60) not null,
  co_code             VARCHAR2(60),
  excutor             VARCHAR2(60),
  excutor_name        VARCHAR2(100),
  input_date          DATE,
  supplier            VARCHAR2(60),
  supplier_name       VARCHAR2(200),
  co_name             VARCHAR2(200),
  su_bank_account     VARCHAR2(200),
  su_bank             VARCHAR2(200),
  su_bank_shoukuanren VARCHAR2(200),
  nd                  VARCHAR2(10),
  dd_sum              NUMBER,
  remark              VARCHAR2(1000),
  status              VARCHAR2(10),
  dd_name             VARCHAR2(200),
  process_inst_id     NUMBER,
  bi_sum              NUMBER,
  su_link_man         VARCHAR2(200),
  su_link_tel         VARCHAR2(200),
  dd_type             VARCHAR2(10)
)
tablespace UFGOV
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );

)

  );

(
  dd_code        VARCHAR2(60) not null,
  dd_item_code   VARCHAR2(60) not null,
  item_content   VARCHAR2(60),
  remark         VARCHAR2(60),
  item_total_sum NUMBER(16,2),
  item_val       NUMBER(16,2) default 0.00,
  item_bi        NUMBER(16,2) default 0.00,
  item_other     NUMBER(16,2) default 0.00,
  item_type      VARCHAR2(20),
  item_detail    VARCHAR2(60)
)
tablespace ZFCG
  pctfree 10
  initrans 1
  maxtrans 255
  storage
  (
    initial 64K
    minextents 1
    maxextents unlimited
  );
